 <a onclick=\"showFmfDescript()\"><h2>About Findmyfare <i class=\"fa fa-chevron-down\"></i></h2> </a>\n\n            <div hidden=\"\" id=\"findmyfare_desc\">\n\n                <h3>Sri Lanka's Largest Online Travel Company</h3>\n\n                <p>\n                    Plan your next vacation with the first and largest online travel company in Sri Lanka findmyfare.com and be ready for some exciting offers. As a fully fledged travel solutions provider we guarantee to offer you the cheapest flight tickets and the lowest hotel reservation packages to suit all your travel requirements.We give you more reasons to visit your favourite city or take that well deserved vacation by offering the lowest fares for flight tickets abroad and the best hotel deals you will find in around the world. When you make your reservation with us our reputation travels with you that is exactly why we offer the hottest prices, the number one service and diverse solutions to plan out your perfect holiday.\n\n                    Findmyfare.com, leading travel portal in Sri Lanka, allows you to search, compare and select the flight you want with a just a few clicks. You can also select from a range of cheap hotels in Sri Lanka or enjoy special discounts on our hotel packages. We work with both premium and budget airlines catering to the needs of high end travelers who prefer luxury International travel packages as well as those who prefer to travel within a budget. Whatever your travel itinerary maybe our focus is to offer you the best fares in the market with unmatched service standards. Our aim is to paradigm online travel solutions in Sri Lanka since the concept that is more common in the world is alien to the local fraternity. \n\n                    All payments for reservations will be done online whilst our customer service staff is available for verbal communication and we ensure hundred percent safe and secure payment gateways that will be directly linked to your respective bank or financial company. The only challenge our customers have in working with us is to find a lower price than what we offer on findmyfare, and if you do we will provide a further discount on your payment, and that's a guarantee! Find out more about the strength of our parent company and comprehensive details about findmyfare.com on About Us page.\n\n                </p>\n            </div>\n\n        </div>\n\n\n        <div
